Label--panel">On this day</h4><div class="Item-content"><div class="Dip Item-dip"><p>In <b>1522</b>, after the death of Magellan who had begun the expedition, Juan Sebastian del Cano completed the first circumnavigation of the world; in <b>1666 </b>the Great Fire of London was extinguished; in <b>1879 </b>the first public telephone exchange in Britain opened in Lombard Street, London; in <b>1901 </b>William McKinley, the 25th American president (1897-1901), was shot in Buffalo, New York, leading to his death eight days later; in <b>1940 </b>King Carol II of Romania abdicated; in <b>1948 </b>Princess Juliana became Queen of the Netherlands after the abdication of her mother; in <b>1968 </b>Swaziland gained its independence from Britain; in <b>1997 </b>Diana, Princess of Wales, was buried in the grounds of Althorp, Northamptonshire.</p> </div></div></div></div><div class="Item DUR-2"><div class="Item-media"><img src="/d/img/DUR-nature-80d36dd1cd.png" alt="Nature notes"></div><div class="Item-content"><h4 class="Item-headline Headline Headline--light Headline--m">Nature notes</h4><div class="ShowMore"><div class="Dip Item-dip Item-dip--withDropcap ShowMore-container js-showMore--dur2a is-hidden"><p>A remarkable small bird now to be seen along our coasts is the little stint. It is a wader no bigger than a great tit, but it flies annually from Siberian marshes to southern Africa, and back again in the spring. It feeds with other waders on beaches and is easily picked out because it is so small. It runs about very quickly on the sand, not probing for food like other waders, such as dunlins, but briskly picking small items up from the surface as it goes. It scarcely ever looks up, so it can be easy to approach. The adults in autumn are a fairly uniform streaky grey above and white below. However, many of these migrants are juvenile birds and can be distinguished by the white “V” on their backs. The female may make the most of the short Arctic summer by laying two clutches of eggs, leaving the first one to the male to incubate, while getting on with the second one.</p> <p class="Byline Byline-name">Derwent May</p></div><div class="Section-footer "><div class="ButtonContainer js-buttonContainer"><button data-tracking='{"event_navigation_name":"button:show more","section_details":"section:nature notes","other_details":"content segment:2"}'  class="Button Button--expand Item-button js-buttonShowMore ShowMore-button js-tracking" data-identifier="dur2a">Show more</button></div></div></div></div></div><div class="Item DUR-2"><div class="Item-media"><img src="/d/img/DUR-birthdays-94b2272911.png" alt="Birthdays"></div><div
